Donc cum es complida la tua inscizio e es remauguda tota aquela carn, lahoras omple le huel de sal trissa, o destilla en lu polvera roga e semblantz a lu de las medicinas corrossivas, e pausa sobre le huel deforo coto am album de huou entro que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	When your incision is complete and all that flesh has been sutured, now fill the wound with finely ground salt, or sprinkle on it red powder resembling corrosive medicines, and place over the wound externally a piece of cloth soaked in egg white until it is ensured free from inflammation.
E si roman alcuna causa de alguardenici e es senhoragat sanc caut, e temes apostema caut, lahoras leyssa le huel e cura aquela apostema am aquo que ceda aquela apostema, e aprop itera sobre aquel am operacio entro que sia sanat, e semblantment fay en la carn ajustada la qual accideys en le huel de aquesta especia.	And if any cause for watchfulness remains and the bleeding is copious, and you fear an abscess may form, then leave the wound open and treat that abscess with whatever relieves it, and then repeat over it as needed until it is healed, and similarly deal with the flesh attached where this type of wound occurs.
Mays empero tu cove que alienes tota curacio del huel freul per via natural o per via accidental, obran am ferr, e no metas la tua ma en alcuna de aquestas operacios entro que veges que aquel membre sia suffertant aquela operacio.	However, you must ensure that all treatment of the wound is done either by natural means or accidentally through the use of tools, and do not put your hand into any of these procedures until you see that the member can sufficiently endure such an operation.
Capitol .xviii.	Chapter XVIII.
De colleccio de sabel en le huel.	On the collection of blood in the wound.
Sabel so venas rogas las quals son testudas sobre le huel e prohibeysso al vesement la sua operacio, e develican le huel am longitut de dias.	Blood comes from toughened veins which lie over the wound and hinder proper treatment, and it can prolong the healing of the wound for many days.
Donc necessari es al comensament que tu consideres si le huel en le qual es sabel es fort e en lu no es autra malautia que sabel, lahoras tu colligeys aquel sabel.	Therefore, at the beginning, it is necessary that you determine if the wound in which there is blood is strong and there is no other illness besides the blood, then you should collect that blood.
E es que tu comandes al malaute que pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop suspen aquelas venas am un onci o am dos segon la tua prudencia; e sia aquel onci de subtil duplicacio segon aquesta forma:	And you command the patient to rest their head on your thigh, and then suspend those veins with an ounce or two according to your judgment; and let that ounce be of fine twofold according to this form:
o so dos oncis gradantment en un cos segon aquesta forma:	Or use two ounces gradually in one course according to this method:
E aprop sian colligidas aquelas venas am forses subtils, am subtilitat, e abstergeys le sanc hora aprop hora, entro que vegas aquelas venas esser remaugudas del huel e sian revolgudas.	And then gather those veins with fine threads carefully, and wipe the blood little by little until you see those veins become free of mucus and are turned inside out.
E guarda te que tu no ledes le huel am las extremitatz del spatum; e si’ la tua operacio en le miegjorn denant le solelh, e sias mot ferm en la tua operacio que no inscidas sino aquelas venas.	And be careful not to lead the mucus with the tips of the spatula; and if your operation is in the middle of the day under the sun, be firm in your operation so that you only incise those veins.
E quan tu auras complitz, lahoras tu distilla en le huel cief vert o rog per que am sa acuitat corrodesca aquo que es remaugut del sabel.	And when you have completed this, then distill into the mucus some clear or red liquid so that its acidity can corrode what is stuck from the scab.
Mays si aquo no es a tu possible colligeys tot en aquela hora, e lahoras tu emplastra tot am aquo que cede la dolor de lu, e leyssa lu per alcus dias entro que sia sedada la dolor de lu e que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	But if you cannot gather everything in that hour, then apply a plaster with something that reduces the pain, and leave it for several days until the pain is subdued and to ensure there is no risk of abscess.
E aprop itera sobre lu segon que la mateyssa manieyra entro que sia sanat.	And then repeat the same procedure on the second area until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de las forfexs:	And this is the form of the forceps:
Capitol .xix.	Chapter XIX.
De reduccio de arizati al nas.	For the reduction of nasal fractures.
Quan tu curas arisati am cauteri o am medicina aguda comburent segon que es precedida la narracio de lu e no es sanat, lahoras no es engen en lu sino que fendas sobre le apostema deves la maturitat de lu, e que extraguas tota la humiditat la qual es en lu e·l poyre entro que sia descubert le os.	When you treat abscesses with cautery or sharp medicine according to what was previously stated in the narration and it is not healed, then do not generate anything inside him but rather make incisions over the abscess until its maturity, and extract all the moisture that is within it along with the pus so that the bone is uncovered.
E donc cum es descubert le os e vezes en lu corrupcio o negror, lahoras tu ratz lu am un sturment del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then when the bone is uncovered and there is corruption or blackening in it, then scrape it with an instrument that has the following form: 
E es nompnat de aspre cap, e sia feyt de fer indi, e sia le cap redon ayssi cum asir le qual sia fayt punctat per punctacio de lima o aliskalfati per punctacio subtil (ayssi cum es en la forma seguent).	E es nompnat de aspre cap, e sia feyt de fer indi, e sia le cap redon ayssi cum asir le qual sia fayt punctat per punctacio de lima o aliskalfati per punctacio subtil (ayssi cum es en la forma seguent).
E pausa aquel sobre le loc corrumput del os, e aprop revolveys aquel entre les tieus ditz, e prem la tua ma petit a petit entro que sapias que aquela corropcio es rasa.	And place that over the corrupted area of the bone, then rotate it between your fingers, and press your hand little by little until you know that the corruption is scraped away.
E aquo sia fayt alcunas veguadas, e aprop restaura le loc am causas exsiccativas e stipticas.	And this should be done several times, and then restore the area with drying and styptic causes.
Donc si·l loc es consolidat e es en lu nascuda bona carn e es abscindit le cors de la sania e roman per xl dias, e no es renovat e no es apostemat e no accideys en lu accident, lahoras tu sapias que es sanat.	Therefore, if the area is consolidated and good flesh has formed and the body has separated from the pus and remains so for forty days, and it does not recur, and there is no abscess and no accidents occur, then you know that it is healed.
E sino, lahoras no es en lu engen sino reduzir la fissura a la forma del nas, e segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu descuebras de segon os am ferr o am medicina acuta, e cum sira descubert le os, lahoras tu pren tribo segon aquesta forma:	And if not, then the goal is not to generate anything but to reduce the fracture to its original form, and according to this method: you must expose the bone using fire or sharp medicine, and once the bone is exposed, take a splint in the following manner:
Sia la extramitat de lu ferr triangulada, e·l fust de lu sia prim extenuat entro a la extremitat ayssi cum vezes assi.	The tip of the iron should be triangular, and the shaft should be gradually tapered towards the end in such a way.
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le os, e sia aquel prop del lacrimal; e alongua la tua ma un pauc del huel, e aprop revol la tua ma am le tribo entro que penetre tot le os, e aquel sente le malaute per asso que atroba vent yssir per so quan te la sua ma.	And then place that over the bone, near the lacrimal area; extend your hand slightly from the wound, and then rotate your hand with the splint until it penetrates the entire bone, causing the patient to feel some air escaping when you hold their hand.
Donc lahoras restaura le loc am medicinas stipticas exsiccantz ayssi cum t’e eyssenhat.	Therefore, now restore the area with astringent and drying medicines as has been mentioned.
Donc cum nays la carn e·l loc es endurazit, lahoras la materia la qual effundia a las partidas deforo retorna al nas, donc aquo es pus leugier sobre le malaute.	Therefore, when the flesh and the area have hardened, the material that was flowing out to the outer parts returns inward, thus this makes the condition lighter on the patient.
Capitol .xx.	Chapter XX.
De reduccio de la eminencia del huel.	On the reduction of a protrusion in the eye.
Quan le huel emineys am la sua totalitat e no accideys en le vezement nocument ni diminuacio, lahoras cove que laxas le malaute, e aprop que·l segues, e aprop que pausas ventozas en le cervitz ses scarificacio e succa per bona succaccio; e aprop pausa sobre le huel liniment le qual sia fayt de acatra e aloe e enses e sarcocolla, e aprop strenh le emplaustre sobre le huel am motz polvils.	When the eye protrudes entirely and does not result in any damage or reduction to the vision, then you should first relax the patient, and subsequently apply bloodletting at the neck with scarification and good suction; and then place an ointment over the eye that is made from acacia, aloe, honey, and tragacanth, and finally secure the poultice on the eye with powdered lint.
E la manieyra dels polvils es que prenguas draps de li leons motz, e quascun drap sia duplicat en quatre plecs; e fay de aquels motz.	And the method for the lint is to take linen cloths and cut them into pieces, and each piece should be folded into four layers; and make use of those cut pieces.
E aprop pausa aquels la un sobre le autre segon la quantitat de la qual ha le huel necessitat.	And then place those one over the other according to the amount that the wound needs.
E aprop strenh sobre aquels am drap dur am fort strictura; e itera las ventosas am succio ses scarificacio; e aprop osta las ventosas e leyssa le huel streyt le dia e la nueyt.	And then press on those with a hard cloth with strong binding; and repeat the cupping with suction and scarification; and then remove the cups and leave the wound exposed day and night.
Mays si entretant le liguament es mollificat, lahoras cove que sia mot streyt.	But if the bandage becomes softened, then it must be made tight again.
E aprop osta le liament aprop le dia e la nueyt ayssi cum havem dit.	And then remove the bandage day and night as we have said.
E si vezes le huel ja esser redusit, bo es, e sino, lahoras itera le emplastre am les polvils e la strictura e las ventosas entro que sia sanat.	And if you find the wound already reduced, it is good, and if not, then repeat the poultice with the powders and binding and cupping until it is healed.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De la inscizio de la eminencia de la tunica uvea.	On the incision of the uveal part of the eye.
Quan endeve disrupcio en la tunica uvea, e aprop es eminent e procezeys fora las palpebras ayssi cum un gra de rasim, e es orrazada la forma de home per aquo, e vols aquo inscidir, lahoras la operacio en lu es ayssi cum havem recomtat, que tu entrometas la agula en la razitz de la uvea de la partida dejos en la partida desus, e aprop met la agula autra en la qual sia fil doble de la part del lacrimal, e fay aquela penetrar e leyssa la primieyra agula segon la sua disposicio; e aprop inscideys le loc del fiel doble e leva am aquel la partida de la uvea en le circuit de la agula, e strenh aquela mot.	When there is disruption in the uveal part of the eye and it becomes prominent and protrudes from the eyelids like a grape of raisin, and takes on the shape of a human figure due to this, and you want to incise this, then the operation is as we have recounted: you insert the needle at the base of the uvea from below upwards, and then place another double-threaded needle in the lacrimal part, and make that penetrate while keeping the first needle in its position; and then incise the area where the double thread is located and lift with it the part of the uvea around the circumference of the needle, and press it firmly.
E aprop extratz la agula e pausa sobre le huel lana infusa en album de huou e leyssa entro que cayha le fil am la uva.	And then remove the needle and place over the wound wool infused in egg white, and leave until the thread comes out with the grape.
E aprop cura le huel am aquo que conforte aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And then treat the wound with something that strengthens it internally so that the ailment may be healed.
E alcunas veguadas aduna de tota partida am cercle de drap entro le huel ajuste eminencia gran, e aprop sia perforat am le spatum subtil que vengua al preon del huel, e corra la humiditat albuginea, e descen le huel e intra tantost.	And sometimes, gather from all sides with a circle of cloth around the swollen wound, and then pierce it with a fine spatula to reach the core of the wound, allowing the whitish moisture to flow out, and reduce the swelling, making it subside immediately.
E aprop strenh entro que sia sanat.	And then strengthen it internally so that it may heal.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXII.
De curacio de alconati.	On the treatment of hernias.
Aquesta malautia que es apelada alconati no es sino sania la qual es ajustada en le huel semblant a aygua dessendent e no es aquela.	This illness, which is called hernia, is nothing but a swelling that appears in the groin, resembling descending water, but it is not that.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en ela es que fasses le malaute sezer sobre la sela aparelada e dreyta, e aprop pren le cap sieu en las tuas mas de doas partz e mau aquel entro que veias la sania pervenir a las partidas dejos, e aprop sia siccada e no descenda, e sia ostat le lum, e·l malaute veia las causas ayssi cum vezia.	The method of treating it is to have the patient sit on a prepared and straight chair. Then take his head in both of your hands and press internally where you see the swelling coming out on either side. Then dry it so that it does not descend, and leave it like this, with the patient seeing the causes just as they appeared.
E si no descendra en jos, sapias que es aygua.	And if it does not descend downward, know that it is water.
Mays si no es preparat le descendement a la sania am aquo que havem dit, lahoras fay le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e aprop pren spatum subtil e fen am aquel sobre le pannicol cernent un petit deves la continuacio de la conjunctiva am la tunica cornea en la corona (entro al loc vuet), entro que sia fora-getada la sania.	And if the pus does not drain properly as we have said, then place the patient between your hands and take a fine spatula, and use it to separate the panniculus from the continuation of the conjunctiva with the corneal tunic at the margin (inside the eye socket), until the pus is completely expelled.
Donc cum es fora-getada, lahoras tu distilla en le huel aygua cauda en la qual has mesclat mel o aygua en la qual ja has bulit fenugrec e mel.	Once it is completely expelled, then you should instill warm water into the nose, in which you have mixed honey, or water in which you have boiled fenugreek and honey.
E aprop sia curat am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And then it should be treated with other methods until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXII.
De la curacio de la aygua descendent del huel.	On the treatment of water (discharge) descending from the nose.
Ja havem dit las specias de la aygua en la divisio e qual conveneys a perforar am sermo declarant, lahoras aquel segon la sanetat.	We have already mentioned the types of discharge in the division and which ones require piercing with clear explanation, according to the health condition.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre un cayrat e lia le sieu huel sa, lu mot stringent.	Now you must place the patient between your hands on a chair and tie their nose tightly with a binding agent.
E aprop pausa prop de la palpebra del sieu huel la tua ma senestra, si le huel en le qual es l’aygua es le huel senestra; o am la tua ma dreyta, si le huel es le dextre.	And then place your left hand near the eyelid of his eye if the affected eye is the left one; or use your right hand if the eye is the right one.
E aprop am la tua ma dextra pren almagda, si le huel es senestre; o am la tua ma senestra, si le huel es de dreyt.	And then use your right hand to take an almond if the eye is the left one; or use your left hand if the eye is the right one.
E aprop pausa la extremitat de almagda prop de la corona per la grossesa del ray en le album del huel de part del mendre lacrimal, e aprop enpelleys almagda am vertut e revol la tua ma am aquel.	And then place the tip of the almond near the crown along the thickness of the ray in the white part of the eye near the smaller tear duct, and then apply the almond with force and rotate your hand in that manner.
E aprop penetre en le album del huel e sentas que almagda ja es pervenguda a causa vueda.	And then penetrate into the white part of the eye and feel that the almond has already reached the desired location.
E cove que sia la masura del cami de almagda al preon la mesura del spazi le qual es de la pupilla entro a la fi de la negror, e es la corona del huel; quar tu veyras am aquel pupilla am la visio de l’huel per la clartat de la tunica cornea.	And it is necessary that the length of the path of the almond to the front be the same as the distance from the pupil to the end of the black part, which is the crown of the eye; for you will see the pupil with the vision of the eye through the clarity of the cornea.
E aprop pausa almagda entro al loc en le qual es l’aygua, e aprop tu la atira en jos una veguada aprop autra, e donc si la aygua descen tantost, lahoras vetz le malaute aquo sobre le qual huebre la sua vista tantost, e almagda en le sieu huel.	And then place the almond in the location where the fluid is, and then pull it down once and then again; if the fluid descends quickly, you will see the patient regain their sight immediately, with the almond still in their eye. 
E aprop repausa se un pauc; donc si la aygua es descenduda, lahoras tu depausa aquela autre veguada abantz que almagda ne sia getada.	And then rest for a while; if the water has drained down, then you wait another interval before any ointment is applied.
E donc quan es sicada e no descen, lahoras tu extrat almagda am facilitat, e revol am aquel la tua ma pauc a pauc, e aprop dissolveys en l’aygua un petit de sal clara de gemma e am aquela lava le huel dedintz; e aprop pausa fora le huel coto o stopa o lana infusa en oli rozat e album de huou e ligua am aquo le huel sa.	And then when it is cut and does not descend, you extract the ointment easily, and rotate your hand slowly with that; then dissolve a little clear gem salt in water and wash the hole inside with it; then place outside of the hole a plug or stopper or wool soaked in anointed oil and egg white and glue with this the hole shut.
Mays nos e aquels que so de nostre temps pause sobre aquel comi trissat am album de huou.	But we and those of our time place upon that wound something crushed with egg white.
E si no obezeys a tu almagda al intrament de l’huel per la sua duricia — quar es alcu dels homes del qual le huel es dur mot —, lahoras cove que prenguas le spatum le qual es nompnat alberid del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if the ointment does not adhere to the interior of the wound due to its hardness—since there are some people for whom the wound is very hard—then you must take the spatula named alberid, which has the following form:
E donc perfora am aquel aquela conjunctura, e no ultimes la tua ma en le trauc, e no es si no que fassas via ad almagda loc subtil.	And then pierce that joint with it, and do not keep your hand in the wound for too long, but only make a fine place for the ointment.
E aprop entromet almagda segon que havem dit.	And then insert the suppository as we have said.
E deves le compliment de la tua obra, sia preparat al malaute dormitori descentment fayt en le qual dorma sobre le sieu dos en mayson tenebrosa, e sia prohibit de totz movementz .	And complete your work by preparing the patient's sleeping area properly, in which they should sleep on their back in a dark room, and all movements are prohibited.
E pausa en la natura de lu aquo per que sia linida la sua natura, e no maugua le sieu cap a la partida dreyta ni senestra de tot.	And pause to understand the nature of the condition so that you can align their natural state, and do not turn their head to the right or left at all.
E sia le liament segon la sua disposicio entro al tertz dia.	And apply the dressing according to its preparation within the third day.
E aprop deslia aquel en aquela maysso tenebrosa e exproha la freol vista, e fay li vezer alcunas causas, e aprop retorna le liament entro al dia .vii.	And then remove that [likely referring to a dressing or bandage] in that dark room and expose it to fresh air, and show him some causes [possibly referring to explaining the reasons], and then reapply the dressing within seven days.
E no cove que fassas aquo en la hora de las curacios o tantost aprop la infusio.	And it is not necessary to do this during the time of treatments or right before the infusion.
Habantz cove que tu alienes aquo per so quar la aygua puega leugierament per gran e vehement de reguardament.	However, it is necessary that you dilute this so that the water can gently pass through, considering it is strong and potent.
Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras cove que deslias le huel denant le vii dia, e rectifica aquel am aquo que ceda apostema.	But if an abscess forms and you need to cauterize it, then you must remove the dressing before the seventh day, and treat it with something that reduces the abscess.
Lahoras tu absol la vista de lu e pausa sobre la cara de lu oral per le qual sia regit le vezement de lu dejos lu per alcus dias, lu existent en la mayszo tenebrosa.	Here is the translation of the given sentence:
E aprop sia gitat de aquela mayzo gradantment e conversa8 en las suas causas.	And then it is gently lowered from that position and turned onto its causes.
E sapias que in alchatea no es excusat le discipol de visio alcunas veguadas, e lahoras tu sias ardit sobre la operacio.	And know that in surgery it is not exempt for the student to see certain things several times, and then you must be bold during the operation.
E ja es pervengut a nos de alcu de aquels les quals so al Artach , e alcu disse que fayt foc en al Ayrac magdaam perforat am le qual es succada la aygua.	And it has been reported to us by some of those who are in the Artach, and some said that fire is made in an Ayrac vessel which is pierced so that water is sucked up.
Mays empero yeu non e vist degu en la nostra terra le qual haia perfeyt aquo, ni e aquo legit en alcu dels libres dels antics; e es possible que aquo sia novel.	But however I have not seen anyone in our land who has perfected this, nor have I read this in any of the books of the ancients; and it is possible that this is new.
E aquestas so las formas de las specias de magdaan per que sia sobre aquelas aquel le qual ignora aquelas:	And these are the forms of the species of medicines for which it is upon those who ignore them:
E sian faytas de eram o de ferr propriament, e sian las extramitatz de lor am aquesta subtilitat triangulada, la extremitat aguda ayssi cum aquela es la forma.	And let them be made of iron or of proper steel, and let the extremities of them have this triangular subtlety, the sharp end thus as that is the form.
Capitol .xxiv.	Capitol .xxiv.
De la curacio de carn nada en le nas.	Of the treatment of flesh hanging from the nose.
Quan en le nas so nascudas carns diversas ajustadas de las quals es alcuna causa la qual es assemblada a scorpio de motz pes, o a polip peys; e aquesta malautia es apelada polipus quar es a semblansa de aquel peys representat.	When on the nose there are various growths of flesh, some of which are caused by a mixture similar to moist scabs or nasal polyps; and this illness is called polypus because it resembles that type of growth.
E de lu es carn cancrosa, lapadea, de fusca color; e de lu es que es carn leon no de color fusca.	And if it is cancerous flesh, it appears pale and of a dark color; and if it is non-cancerous flesh, it is not of a dark color.
Donc en aquela que es en aquestas carns leon no fraudulenta ni cancroza, cove que fassas le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e posat al solelh, e huebre las nars de lu, e picoys le tieu onci en aquelas carns.	Therefore, in those cases where the flesh is not fraudulent nor cancerous, you should have the patient sit between your hands and expose them to the sun, clean their nostrils, and pierce the area with a needle in those fleshy parts.
E aprop extrat aquela a las partidas deforo, e aprop inscindeys aquo que has comprehendut de aquelas am spatum agut subtil de la una partida entro que sapias que tota la carn ja es ostada; que si roman de lu deguna causa de la qual la abscisio es possibla, lahoras tu ratz aquo am la un dels estrumentz subtils am facilitat entro que de lu romangua denguna causa.	Then extract it from the outer parts, and then divide what you have grasped of those areas with a sharp and fine spatula inserted into one part until you know that all the flesh has been removed; because if any part remains which could cause separation to be possible, then you scrape it with one of the fine instruments easily until nothing remains that could cause any issue.
Mays si senhoreja am sanc o accida apostema caut, lahoras tu pausa a lu aquo que cove; o es dels apostemas malignes, lahoras tu coyta e cauteriza aquel entro que sia abscindit sanc e sian ostadas las cavas totas.	If it is ruled by blood or an abscessed swelling appears, then you apply what is necessary; if it is one of the malignant swellings, then you cut and cauterize that area where blood needs to be severed and all the veins removed.
E aprop sia getatz en le nas aprop la inscizio vi agre e aygua o vi.	And then pour into the nose near the beginning something agreeable and mixed with water or wine.
Mays si le nas es ubert e de lu procezeys humiditat entro al palat, lahoras sapias que ja es sanat.	But if the nose is open and you process humidity into the palate from it, then know that it is already healed.
Mays si la humiditat no penetra segon que cove, lahoras tu sapias que dedintz lu es carn nada en los pus sobiras osses de las nars als quals non es pervengut abscizio.	But if the humidity does not penetrate as it should, then you know that inside there is flesh mixed with pus over the bones of the nose to which incision has not been successful.
Donc lahoras cove que entromitas fiel de li al qual sia alcuna grosseza, e nuza en lu motz nuzes, e pausa entre quascun nutz la quantitat del dit o mens, e engene le malaute e entromet una extremitat del fiel en le nars am lo ray o am autra causa la qual es a lu possibla.	Therefore, now it is necessary to insert a thread into the nose where there is some thickness, and place crushed nuts on it, placing between each nut an amount equal to the width of a finger or thumb, and prepare the patient and insert one end of the thread into the nose with the aid of a reed or another suitable instrument.
E pus que aquo aura fayt, que atire le sieu odorament entro que pervengua a las canals de las nars, e sia eyssit sobre le sieu golayro, quar tropas veguadas le semblant ad aquesta accio fan les enfantz a las scolas, e es leugiera causa ad aquel que ho vol far.	And after this has been done, draw his own odor inward so that it reaches the nasal passages, and sit on his pillow, for children often mimic this action at school, and it is an easy method for those who wish to perform it. 
E aprop pausa las dos extramitatz del fiel, una extremitat que iesca sobre le nas et l’autra que romangua en le nas, e aprop aministra serratura de carn am les nuzes que so en le fiel, e fay aquo entro que sapias que las carn ja so am les nuzes del fiel.	And then place the two ends of the splint, one end that comes over the nose and the other that remains on the nose, and then apply a suturing of flesh with the knots that are in the splint, and do this until you know that the flesh is already secured with the knots of the splint. 
E aprop extratz le fiel, e pausa en le nas aprop la abstraccio del sanc una calgua , e fay aquo per tres dias o mays entro que l’enguent corrodo tot aquo que es romas de las carns.	And then extract the bile, and place near the nostrils during bloodletting a sponge, and do this for three days or more until the poultice corrodes all that is rotten in the flesh.
E aprop en la fi de la causa, pausa en le nas una canula de plom per alscus jorns entro que sia sanat.	And at the end of the treatment, place a lead cannula in the nose for several days until it is healed.
Mays si endigeys de curacio que exsique, usa de aquela.	And if you finish the treatment and it dries up, use that method. 
E aquesta es la forma del instrument a capipurge fazedor am le qual son distillatz olis e medicinas en le nars:	And this is the form of the instrument used for purging with which oils and medicines are distilled into the nose:
E fay aquo de argent o de eram, la qual sia semblant a una petita lampesa uberta, ayssi cum petita conqua, e le meat semblantment.	And do this with silver or amber, which should resemble a small open lantern, like a little shell, and the meat similarly.
E si vols, fay una canula clausa ayssi cum cana, e la cancula del estrument a capipurge fazedor e sia plana, descuberta; a la qual sia manubre en lo derier de lu, am le qual tenguas aquela quan escaufas en lu oli o aquo que tu vols dels sucs e de las causas suctiblas.	And if you want to, make a closed tube like a cane, and the part of the instrument for purging should be open and flat; which should be placed at the back of the patient, with which you hold it when you heat it in oil or whatever other substances and suctionable causes you wish.
E aquestz capipurgi es precios: recipe de enforbi de castor, de balayra blanc, de giengiebre, e piletre de safra, de pebre lonc, de escafragia, de epetum de spic ana unc. vi cumfizeys am suc de bleda e de caul, e sian faytas pillulas, e sia destemprada una pillula am aygua tebeza, e sia gitat en las nars del malaute jasent envers.	And these capipurgi are precious: take castoreum, white balm, ginger, saffron crocus, long pepper, scammony, and thyme in equal parts by the uncia (ounce). Mix them with the juice of leek and onion, make pills from them, dissolve one pill in warm water, and administer it into the nostrils of the patient lying down.
Capitol .xxv.	Chapter XXV.
De theyls natz en las extramitatz del nas.	About nasal polyps in the outer parts of the nose.
Motas veguadas es nat theyl en las extramitatz del nas, e es magnificat e omentat en alscus dias entro en que mot es leg le reguardament de lu.	White spots appear as polyps in the outer parts of the nose, and they grow and change within a few days, during which time their condition should be monitored.
E per aquo cove que tu inscidas aquel en le comensament de la apparissio de lu, e erediques tot aquel.	And because of this, you should incise it at the beginning of its appearance and remove all of it.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc o cauteri o medicina comburent la qual estia en loc de lu.	Then place a cautery or a burning medicine on the area where it was removed.
Mays si es tardada la sua inscizio entro que sia magnificat, lahoras considera si es lapificat, dur, de fusca color e de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr quar es apostema crancos; quar motas veguadas ad aquel que inscideys aquesta apostema endeve per lu granda malicia sobre aquel le qual aquel havia.	But if the incision is delayed until it has grown larger, then consider whether it has become calcified, hard, dark in color, and less sensitive. In this case, do not touch it with iron, for it may be a chronic abscess; because sometimes one who incises such an abscess can cause great harm to the area that was affected.
E si le apostema es de leon tocament e no es de fosca color, e vezes que inscizio es possibla en tot aquel, lahoras evacua le malaute e inscideys aquel senes temor, e cura le loc am aquo que exsique e costrenh entro que sia sanat.	And if the abscess is of a light touch and not of a dark color, and when incision is possible in all of it, then evacuate the patient and incise that without fear, and treat the area with something that dries and constrains until it is healed.

De sutura del nas e de las labias e de la aurelha quan la continuitat es dissolvuda per plagua o per semblantz.	On缝合鼻子、嘴唇和耳朵当它们因伤或类似原因而断裂。
Sapias que quan accideys solucio de continuitat en una de aquestas cartillages, pauc confereys en aquela operacio sino en alcus homes.	Understand that when you encounter a rupture of continuity in one of these cartilages, you should not place much confidence in that operation unless it is in certain men.
Donc cove, quan endeve ad alcu alcuna causa de aquelas, que consideres si es plagua fresca am le sieu sanc, e lahoras tu ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, when you encounter any cause of those wounds, you should consider if it is a fresh wound with its own blood, and then you align the two edges of the wound with sutures, and then care for the inside so that it heals.
E si las labias de solucio de continuitat so ja separadas, e quascuna es fayta sana, lahoras cove que tu excorjes quascuna partida de la sua codena apparent entro que n’iesca sanc.	And if the edges of the wound that has broken continuity are already separated and each is made whole, then you must pull each part of its visible stitches until blood comes out.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias am sutura e strenh aquelas, e sobre aquelas pulveriza sanc de drago e enses trissat, e pausa sobre la polvera una pessa de emplaustra diafinicon, o de alcu autre dels emplastres consolidatius, e leyssa aquel liat per dos jorns o per tres, e aprop deslia aquel e permuta aquel emplaustre e leyssa aquel entro que·ls fiels per si sian abscinditz, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then adjust the two lips with sutures and tighten them, and sprinkle dragon's blood powder on them which you have ground finely, and place over the powder a piece of diafinicon plaster, or some other consolidating plaster, and leave that bandage for two days or three, and then remove it and replace that plaster until the stitches fall off by themselves, and finally care for it with ointment until it is healed.
Mays la manieyra de la sutura es que tu agregues la solucio de continuitat o am agulhas ayssi cum havem recomtat en la sutura del ventre, o agregua la solucio de continuitat am fiel ayssi cum a tu e fayt saber.	And the method of suturing is that you close the discontinuity with needles as we have recommended in the suturing of the abdomen, or you can also close the discontinuity with stitches as you know how to do.

De extraccio de aquela causas que veno en las doas labias en las partidas dedintz.	On the extraction of those causes that occur in the two lips within the partitions.
Motas veguadas endeve a motz homes en las partidas dedintz de las suas labias alcus apostemas durs semblantz a gras de errs, e alscunas de lors son mendres e alcunas son majors. Capitol .xxix.	Chapter XXIX.
De razo de dentz am ferr.	On the extraction of teeth with force.
Quan en la superficia de las dentz de las partidas dedintz e de las de foro e entre las gingivas so ajustadas escorsas aspras, legas, e alcunas veguadas son de nigradas e son faytas citrinas o vertz entro que a la gingiva ve per aquo corrupcio e son faytas las dentz legas.	When on the surface of the teeth, both those inside and outside, and between the gums, there are sharp splinters, tartar, and some swamps that are blackened or yellowish-green, this leads to corruption in the gum and causes the teeth to become decayed.
E donc cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas e pausar le cap de lu en le tieu se, e ratz las dents en las quals apareysso aquelas escorsas e causas semblantz arena entro que de lor no romangua deguna causa, e aquo fay de la negror e de la citrinitat e de las autras entro que sian mondificadas.	And thus it is necessary that you seat the patient between your hands and place his head on your thigh, and scrape the teeth in which you find those scales and cause similarities to sand so that none of these causes remain, and this is done for the blackness and yellowness and other things so that they may be cleansed.

Capitol .xxx.	Chapter .xxx.
D’eradicacio de dentz.	For the eradication of teeth.
Cove que tu cures la dent de la sua dolor am tot engen e tardes en tota eradicacio de lu, quar no es denguna causa que suplisqua la veguada de lu quan es eradicada, quar es sustancia sublima entro que es excusacio en la eradicacio de lu.	Here is the translation of the provided sentence:
Mays cove quan le malaute es forsat aquela dent eradicar, que fermament deves tu sia certificat quala es la dent dolent, quar motas veguadas la dolor descep le malaute e cuga que sia en dent sana, e tu eradicas aquela e aprop la dolor no cessa entro que la dent malauta e dolent sia eradicada, quar nos ja havem vist aquo per operacio dels barbies.	More importantly, when the patient is forced to have that tooth removed, you must be certain which one is causing pain, because often the pain can deceive the patient and lead them to believe a healthy tooth is the source. If you remove that one and the pain does not stop until the diseased and painful tooth is extracted, for we have already seen this through barber surgeries.
Donc cum deves tu es sertificat qual es la dent dolent, e que o sabes be, lahoras cove que tu scarifiques en le circuit de la dent am spatum en le qual sia alcuna vertut, entro que sia dissolvut de la dent de la gingiva de tota partida, e aprop mau aquel am les tieus ditz, o am forfexs subtils al comensament petit a petit entro que aquela concucesquas.	Therefore, you must be certain which tooth is causing pain, and once you know this well, then you need to scrape around the tooth with a spatula that has some medicinal power, until it separates from the gum completely. Then remove it using your fingers or with fine scissors bit by bit until it comes out.
E aprop alogua en lu fortz tenalhas grans per bona loquacio o estuptura fort, e pausa le cap del malaute entre les tieus denolhs que be le tengues que no·s maugua, e aprop tratz la dent segon rectitut en manieyra que no trenques aquela, ni al malaute major dolor no dones.	And then take large forceps with good gripping power or strong pliers, and hold the patient's head between your knees so that you have a firm grip and it does not move, and then pull the tooth straight out in such a way that you do not break it nor cause greater pain to the patient.
E donc si no es foro-getat, lahoras pren un de aquels instrumentz, e met aquel dejos lu de tota part am facilitat e esforsa la remocio de lu ayssi que es feyt al comensament.	And if it is not easily removed, then take one of those instruments and gently remove it from all sides, exerting effort to extract it in the same manner as at the beginning.
Mays si la dent es trauquada o corrosa, lahoras cove que tu comples de drap aquel trauc e estrenguas aquel am la extremitat de ray subtil per so que no sia trinquada en la hora de la tua constriccio sobre aquela am tenalas.	But if the tooth is loose or decayed, then you must wrap a piece of cloth around the loose part and tighten it with the tip of a fine probe so that it does not break when you apply pressure to it with forceps.
E cove que tu obres exquesitament am scarificacio en le circuit de tota part de la gingiva e guarda mot la tua fortaleza que no trenques aquela e romangua partida de lu, e retorne sobre le malaute per la malicia que sia majo que la primieyra dolor de lu.	And it is necessary that you perform carefully with scarification around all parts of the gum and be mindful of your strength so as not to tear that part and leave a wound, and return to the patient for the harm to be less severe than the initial pain.
E guarda te que no fassas aquo que fan alscus ignorantz barbiers en lor fistinacio e audacia sobre la eradicacio de lor, ses que no aministran aquo que nos havem recomtat; quar motas veguadas fan venir sobre les homes malautias grans las quals son pus dificils que sian trinquadas, e las razitz de lor remaugudas totas, o alcunas de aquelas, o que extrayguas aquela am alcus osses de la mandigula ayssi cum motas veguadas havem testificat.	And be careful not to do what some ignorant barbers do in their stubbornness and audacity regarding the removal of them; for they often bring severe illnesses upon men which are harder to treat, and the roots of which remain unhealed, or that you extract it along with some bones of the jaw as we have testified many times.
E aprop la eradicacio de lu sia lavada la boca am vi caut o vi agre am sal.	And then for the extraction of it, the mouth should be washed with hot wine or sour wine with salt.
E si endeve fluxs de sanc per aysso, ayssi cum motas veguadas endeve, lahoras trissa alcuna quantitat de zegi e aspergeys sobre la plagua, e si no confereys aquel zegi, cauteriza.	And if bleeding occurs because of this, just as it sometimes happens unexpectedly, then sprinkle some amount of zaugy (a kind of medicinal substance) on the wound, and if that zaugy does not work, apply a cautery.
La forma de las forceps e tenalas subtils am las quals es mauguda la dent al comensament sia de longua extramitat, de breu manubre e gros, per so que no sian doblatz quan am aquels deves obrar.	The form of the forceps and delicate tongs with which a tooth is extracted should be long at the end, short in manipulation, and thick, so that they do not bend when using them for this task.
E sian ayssi cum vezes de gros manubre entro que quan estrenhas am aquelas no sian dobladas, sian breus extramitatz.	And they should be thick in the middle so that when you exert force with them, they do not bend, and their ends should be short.
E sian faytas de ferr de India descentment faytas de dreytas extramitatz, e en las extramitatz de aquelas sian dentz de las quals las unas intron en las autras e estrenhan per constriccio descent fort, e alscunas veguadas las extramitatz de aquelas sian la forma del bec d’un auzel le qual ha nom ciconia, so es guanta, e son de fort constriccio.	And they should be made of Indian iron, properly fashioned with straight ends, and at the ends of these, there should be teeth that fit into each other and exert force through strong constriction. Sometimes, the ends of these are in the shape of the beak of a bird called ciconia, which is a stork, and they have a powerful constricting ability.

But the skilled and subtle artisan in the art can find by themselves according to what the operation and diverse diseases indicate; for there are diseases for which the ancients did not describe or leave proper instruments, due to the varied forms of different kinds.

Capitol .xxxii.	Chapter XXXII.
De la cura de las dentz eminentz sobre las autras.	On the treatment of prominent teeth over the others.
Quan las dentz so eminentz no segon lor cors natural per aquelas la forma es laga, e majorment quan endeve a las femnas, e majorment a las piuselas venerablas; donc cove que tu consideras: si dent es nada aprop autra dent, e no es possibla sarradura ni linament de lu, lahoras radica aquela; mays que no sia annexa am autra dent, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am aquest instrument del qual aquesta es la forma; e es semblant a morr de porc, e sia feyt de ferr de India de extramitat mot aguda.	When the prominent teeth do not follow their natural course and are more prone to this condition, especially among women, and particularly those who are more venerable; therefore, you must consider: if a tooth is close to another tooth and cannot be removed or loosened, then extract that one; but if it is not attached to another tooth, then cut it with this instrument, which has the following form; it resembles a pig's snout and should be made of Indian iron with an extremely sharp edge.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscideyses aquela en trops dias per la duricia de la dent, e que no sia comauguda autra de las dentz.	And let your incision be such that you cut it over several days due to the hardness of the tooth, and ensure that none of the other teeth are damaged.
E si es dent eminent expausat a limadura, lahoras lima aquel am lima de ferr de India del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if a prominent tooth is excessively rough, then file it with an Indian iron file, which has the following form:
E sia tot de ferr de India e·l margua eysament; e sia de motz menutz puntz ayssi cum lima am la qual son faytas agulhas, am la qual la dent sia limada pauc a pauc en motz dias am fecilitat, per so que no sia autra dent comauguda e caga.	And it should all be made of Indian iron and the file used carefully; and it should be made of ground points like a file with which needles are made, with which the tooth is filed little by little over several days easily, so that no other tooth becomes damaged or decays.
E aprop lineys aquela en la fi, e ratz aquela am alscus razoris.	And then tie that at the end, and shave that with sharp razors.
E si es dent del qual una partida es trinquada e lideys la lengua, lahoras cove que tu limescas aquel entro que l’aspretat de aquela fraccio sia ostada e engualhada, e sia aplenada per so que la lengua no ledesca ni la paraula no corrumpa.	And if it is a tooth of which a part is broken and it harms the tongue, then you must file that inside so that the roughness of that fragment is removed and smoothed, and fill it so that the tongue is not hurt nor the speech corrupted.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Chapter XXXIII.
De restauracio de dentz maugudas am fiel de aur o de argent.	On the restoration of damaged teeth with gold or silver fillings.
Quan accideys a las dentz devant concussio e remossio per percussio o per cazament, e le malaute no pot strenher sobre aquo que manga, e tu has curat aquel am medicinas stipticas, e no ha valgut la tua curacio, lahoras per so que no cagan es engen en aquelas que sian strengudas am fiel de aur e no de argent, quar argent se fa vert e aprop se poyreys aprop alscus dias, mays aur nul temps no es mudat.	When you encounter front teeth that have been displaced or loosened by impact or falling, and the patient cannot chew on what they eat, and you have treated it with styptic medicines but your treatment has not worked, then in order to prevent them from falling out, they should be secured with gold fillings and not silver ones, because silver can corrode and will fall out after a few days, whereas gold never changes.
E sia le fiel en tal subtilitat e grocesa segon la quantitat que puesca entrar entre las dentz; e la forma de la reccio es que prenguas le fiel e pren lo doble de lu entre doas dentz sanas, e aprop que cresques am doas tortuositatz del fiel entre doas maugudas, o si’ una o motas, entro que pervengua la tela a la dent sana del autra partida.	And the filling should be of such fineness and thickness that it can enter between the teeth; and the method is to take the filling material and place twice as much between two healthy teeth, then increase it with two twists of the filling material between the damaged teeth, or if there is one or several, until the thread reaches the healthy tooth on the other side.
E aprop itera le teyssiment entro a la partida de la qual comenciest, e strenh la tua ma am facilitat e savieza entro que no sia mauguda.	And then repeat the insertion into the area where you began, and insert your hand with ease and skill so that it is not rough.
E sia la tua striccio am la qual strenhas le fiel deves las razitz de las dentz que no evasesca.	And let your grip be with which you hold the thread so that it does not slip from the roots of the teeth.
E aprop inscindeys las extramitatz del fiel superfluens am las forceps o tosoyras, e agregua aquelas en quascun loc am gesti, e converteys aquelas e las occulta entre la dent sana e la dent mauguda, per so que no fassa lesio a la lengua.	And then separate the excess bile from the extremities using forceps or tongs, and add those to each area by hand, and place them between the healthy tooth and the decayed tooth, so that they do not cause injury to the tongue.
E aprop leyssa aquela ayssi streyta cum roman.	And then loosen that area as tightly as possible.
Mays si es desliada o rumpuda, strenh aquela o aquelas am autra fiel en tal manieyra en tot son temps.	If it is loosened or broken, strengthen that or those with another thread in such a manner throughout its entire length. 
E aquesta es la forma de las dentz e la figura de la rectacio de doas dentz sanas e de doas maugudas, ayssi cum vezes aquestas liadas:	And this is the form of the teeth and the figure of the reaction of two healthy teeth and two diseased ones, just as you see these bound together:
E quan se fa que retorno una dent o doas aprop le cazement de quascuna en lors locs, e sian recrescutz ayssi cum havem recomtat, e que remauguan.	And when it is done that one or two teeth are returned to their respective places at the gum line, and they have grown back as we have described, and that they remain in place.
E no fa aquo sino bo artifexs e savi.	And this is done only by skilled artisans and wise [individuals].
E alcunas veguadas es aptat alcuna causa dels osses de vaca, e es fayt de lor ayssi cum forma de dent, e es pausada en loc en le qual defayl la dent, e es strengit ayssi cum havem dit, e reman e serveys am aquel per lonc temps.	And sometimes a piece of cow bone is adapted as a cause [likely meaning "solution" or "remedy"], and it is fashioned into the shape of a tooth, and it is placed in the location where the tooth is missing, and it is secured as we have said, and it remains and serves for a long time.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Chapter XXXIV.
De inscizio del liament le qual ve en la lengua e prohibeys loquela.	On the condition that affects the tongue and prevents speech.
Aquest liguament le qual ve dejos la lengua alcunas veguadas o es natural am le qual hom nays, o accidental e accideys per plagua la qual ja es consolidada.	This condition that affects the tongue sometimes is present from birth, with which a person is born, or it is accidental and occurs due to an injury that has already healed.
E la operacio en lu es que huobres la boca del malaute, le sieu cap existent en le tieu se; e eleva la sieua lengua, e aprop inscideys aquel liament nervos segon la latitut entro que sia solvuda la lengua de la sua recencio.	And the operation is to open the mouth of the patient, with their head positioned in your lap; then lift their tongue, and subsequently cut that nervous ligament according to the width within which the tongue is separated from its root.
Mays si en aquela es alcuna duricia o denodacio, e aquo es stat per consolidacio de plagua, lahoras tu gieta unci e scindeys aquel per la latitut entro que aias inscindit le liament e sia dissolvuda la nodacio.	And if in that area there is any hardness or knotting, and this has been caused by the consolidation of an inflammation, then you cut and divide that area across its width between where you have already divided the ligament and dissolved the knot.
E guarda te que no sia fayta fissura en le preon de la carn e que scindas aqui arceria e vengua flux de sanc.	And take care that a fissure is not made in the layer of flesh and that you do not split the artery here, causing blood to flow.
E aprop sia lavat le vestigi de la inscisio am ayguaros o am vi agre o am aygua frega; e aprop pausa dejos la lengua licini; so es meca la qual tengua le malaute dejos la lengua en quascuna nuoyt per so que no sia consolidat autra veguada.	And then wash the remnants of the incision with wine, or with vinegar, or with cold water; and then place a salve on it; this is a method where the patient keeps the salve under their tongue each night to prevent it from solidifying again. 
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, pausa sobre le loc vetriol trissat; mays si le sanc ventz, lahoras cauteriza le loc am cauteri lantiginos le qual conveneys ad aquo.	And if a blood flow occurs, place finely ground vitriol over the area; but if the bleeding continues, then cauterize the area with a red-hot cautery which is suitable for this purpose.
E aprop aquel cura am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	Then treat it with other methods until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Chapter XXXV.
De extraccio de ranula dejos la lengua.	On the extraction of a ranula from the tongue.
Alcunas veguadas accideys dejos la lengua apostema asemblant a nomla petita prohibent la lengua de la sua operacio natural; e fort leu es magnificada entro que huempla la boca.	Sometimes, a swelling resembling a small ranula appears on the tongue, preventing it from functioning normally; and it grows inside until it fills the mouth.
E la operacio en lu es que huebras la boca del malaute sesent devant le solel e considera le apostema.	And the procedure is to open the mouth of the patient wide in front of the sunlight and examine the swelling.
E si tu le vezes de fusca color o de negra, dur, al qual le malaute no atroba sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel quar es cranc.	And if you see it is of dark or black color, hard, and the patient feels no sensation in it, then do not touch it for it is cancerous.
E si es declinat a blancor, en le qual es humiditat, lahoras tu met le onci en lu, e inscideys aquel am spatum subtil, e inscindeys le de tota partida; e si sanc te ventz en la hora de la tua operacio, lahoras tu pausa desus zegi trissat, so es vetriol, entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if it has turned white, indicating moisture, then insert your finger into it and incise it with a fine spatula, cutting it completely; and if blood flows during the procedure, then place finely ground vitriol on it until the bleeding stops.
E aprop retorna a la obra tua entro que lo haias trayt am compliment de lu, entro que sia lavat am vi agre e sal; e cura aquel am l’autra curacio ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And then return to your work before you have fully taken it out, before it is washed with sweet wine and salt; and treat that with another cure until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Capitol .xxxvi.
De extraccio de apostema de doas aurelhas e de aquel que es nada en le golayro e de las autras apostemas.	From the extraction of abscesses from both ears and those that occur in the throat, as well as other abscesses.
Quan endeveno en le golayro godat, so son glandulas las quals son asembladas algodat, las quals accideysso deforas e son nompnadas doas aurelhas, las quals quan tu las curas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no es sanat, lahoras tu considera si le apostema es dur, de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr.	When they appear in the throat swollen, these are glands that are somewhat similar, which develop outward and are called the tonsils. When you treat them with what we have said in the division and it does not heal, then consider if the abscess is hard, of a dark color, with little sensation, then do not touch it with iron.
E si es de roga color e la razic es grossa, lahoras no toques aquela am ferr per le flux del sanc; abantz layssa aquel entro sia madurat, e lahoras o tu trauqueras aquel, o sira romput per si.	And if it is of a red color and the root is large, then do not touch it with iron due to the flow of blood; before you let it mature inside, then either you will extract it, or it will burst on its own.
E si es de blanqua color, radon, e la razit de lu es subtil, lahoras aquel es que cove esser inscidit.	And if it is of a white color, swollen, and the root is delicate, then that one needs to be incised.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras, denant la tua operacio, si ja ha repausat le apostema de lu caut am repaus complit o si es deminuit am alcuna deminucio; e lahoras fay sezer le malaute denant le soleyl, e·l cap de lu sia en le tieu se, e huebre la boca de lu, e le servidor prenent entre las suas mas prema la lengua de lu dejos am instrument mot noble del qual aquesta es la forma:	And the operation on it is that you consider, before your operation, if the abscess has rested from cautery with complete rest or if it has decreased somewhat; then make the patient sit facing the sun, and his head should be in your hand, and open his mouth, and the servant takes hold of his tongue with an instrument of noble design, which has this form:
E sia fayt de argent o de aram, e sia subtil cum cotel.	And whether it is made of silver or iron, it should be sharp like a knife. 
Donc cum tu premes am aquel la lengua e es mostrat a tu la apostema, e catz sobre aquel le tieu vezement, lahoras pren onci e fica aquel en l’amenla, e tira aquel a las partidas defora tant quant podes.	Therefore, when you press with that the tongue and the swelling is shown to you, and cut on that your garment, then take an ounce and place that in the swelling, and pull that outwards as much as you can.
Otra aquo que tiras alcuna causa de las tunicas, e aprop incideys aquela am instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	And here is the translation of the given line:
e es asemblat a forceps, empero las extramitatz de lu son corvadas, ayssi que l’orrifici de quascuna de aquelas es en le endreyt del autra, mot agudas, le qual sia de ferr indi enbegut.	And it is similar to forceps, but the ends of it are curved, so that the opening of each one is in line with the other, being sharp, which is made of iron and well-tempered.
Mays si aquest instrument no es a tu present, lahoras inscideys aquel am spatum del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: E sia agut de la una part, no agut del autra part.	But if this instrument is not available to you, then cut it with a spatula of which this is the form: It should be sharp on one side and blunt on the other side.
E pus que has inscidit una mella, inscideys l’autra segon aquesta meteyssa manieyra de inscizio, e aprop la inscizio le malaute guarguarise de aygua frega	And after you have incised one thigh, incise the other in the same manner of incision, and then the incision will heal the patient from cold humors.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, guarguarise aygua de decoccio de scorsa de milgrana o de fuelha de mirtra e semblantz ad aquel de las causas stiptiquas entro que·l flux del sanc sia restreyt, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	If there is an excessive flow of blood, use water from the decoction of pomegranate peel or myrtle leaves and similar styptic causes until the bleeding is stopped, then treat it until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas naysso en le guolayro autras apostemas otra aquelas doas aurelhas, e inscideys aquelas segon que yeu e dit en la inscizio de doas mellas engualment.	And at times there appear other swellings in the gums or on those two auricles, and incise those as I have said in the section about incising two tumors similarly.
E yeu ja fu medicat una femna de apostema le qual era nat en le golayro de lu, le qual apostema tendia a color fusca, de pauc sentiment, le qual ja havia claus le golayro de lu, e la femna respirava am meat streyt, e ja havia prohibit a lu comestio e beure de aygua, e ja era pervenguda a la mort si mays agues stat per un dia o per dos.	And I have already treated a woman with an abscess that had formed in her throat, which abscess tended to a dark color, of little sensation, and it had already closed off her throat, the woman was breathing with great difficulty, and had already been deprived of food and water, and she would have reached death if it had lasted one more day or two.
E l’apostema ja tant havia pugat que havia mezes dos ramps entro que eyssiro per dos traucs.	And the abscess had risen so much that it broke through two paths to discharge through two channels.
Donc yeu me cuytegui fisturalment e fiquegui en un de lor onci, e tiregui aquel, e atirada es de lu gran porcio, e aprop yeu incidigui aquela de on comprendegui del autre trau, e aprop yeu obrigui la boca de lu, e compremegui la sua lengua, e aprop yeu fiquegui le onci en aquela apostema.	Therefore, I decided to act surgically and inserted one of the instruments into one of the paths, and pulled it out, and a large portion was expelled. Then I incised the other path where I understood the abscess continued, and then I forced open the mouth, and pressed her tongue, and then I inserted the instrument into that abscess.
E aprop yeu abscizi gran partida de lu, e no corria de lu sino un pauc de sanc.	Then I removed a large part of it, and only a little blood flowed from it.
Donc absolut es le guolayro de aquela femna, e comensec tantost beure aygua, e aprop presec vianda, donc yeu no cessegui inscidir de aquela apostema motas vetz per lonc temps, e succesia apostema en loc de aquel, le qual inscizia entro que es prolonguat aquel.	Therefore, the throat of that woman was cleared, and she immediately began to drink water, and soon after took food. Thus, I did not cease to incise that abscess multiple times for a long time, and new abscesses would form in place of those, which I continued to incise until they were fully resolved.
Donc yeu engen agui e cauterizegui le guolayro de lu, donc astec de addicio; e aprop yeu perambulegui e no saubi que fec Dieus de aquela aprop mi.	Therefore, I have already gathered and cauterized the wound of him, thus stopping the bleeding; then I wandered about and do not know what God did with that one near me.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Capitol .xxxvii.
De inscizio de huvela quan es apostemada.	From the beginning of the swelling when it has become abscessed. 
Quan catarr deysen a la huvula, e es apostemada e es longa, lahoras ela es nompnada perpendicular; e si es en la partida dejos grossa e redonda, e lahoras ela es apelada buba.	When they call it catarrh in the throat, and if it is swollen and elongated, then it is named perpendicular; and if it is found thick and round in a part, then it is called buba. 
Mays quan es curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio, e no comfereys la tua curacio, e eyssament ja vezes que apostema caut ja es ostat de lu e es subtil, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquela que es agreguadas redonda; e si es ad aquela longitut, e es sanguina, de fusca color o de negre, e no es a lu centiment, lahoras cove que tu temtes la inscizio de lu, quar en aquela es temor sobre le malaute.	When it is treated with what we have said in the division, and you do not find your treatment effective, and nevertheless you see that an abscess has already formed and is hardened and subtle, then you must incise around the area that has aggregated; and if it extends to a certain length, and is bloody, of dark or black color, and does not feel sensitive, then you must attempt to incise it, for in this there is fear for the patient.
E quan tu vezes aquela segon la manieyra que yeu he dita de la sua blancor e longuesa, que tu fassas sezer le malaute e premas la lengua de lu am instrument del qual procesic la sua forma e aprop fica le onci en la nuva, e tira aquela en jos e inscideys aquela am un de dos instrumentz les quals e ditz en la inscizio de dos mellas.	And when you see that according to the method I have described of its whiteness and length, you should make the patient sit and press their tongue with an instrument whose shape allows for this procedure, then insert the ounce into the new area, pull it down, and incise it using one of two instruments which are used in the incision of two halves. 
E cove que no inscidas aquela sino aquo que es ajustat sobre le terme natural ses addicio, quar si tu inscides de lu mays, lediyras le sieu parlar.	And it is necessary that you do not incise beyond what naturally fits its boundary, for if you cut further, you will harm their speech.
E aprop la inscizio, usa de aquo le qual havem recomtat en la inscizio de dos mellas, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And then for the incision, use what we have recommended in the section of two halves, and take care that it heals properly.
Mays si era le malaute espaventat per la inscizio de lu, cove que use de engen en la cauterizacio de lu ses temor, e la manieyra del cauteri en lu no es sino am aygua aguda, e es que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop prem la lengua de lu am le instrument le qual havem dit, e aprop pren de l’aygua la qual havem dita en le capitol de cauterizacio, e comfeys am aquela caus viva, e pausa aquela no spessa ni subtil, e de aquela omple la concavitat de l’estrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	If the patient is frightened by the incision made on them, one must use ingenuity in the cauterization to address their fear, and the method of cauterization should not be harsh but rather with sharp water. Place the head of the patient on your thigh, then press their tongue with the instrument we have mentioned, and then take the water that has been specified in the chapter on cauterization, and warm it with that live heat source, and place it neither too thickly nor thinly, and use this to fill the concavity of the instrument which is shaped thus:
Sia la extramitat de lu conquavitat en la qual sia pausada la medicina ayssi cum la conquavitat de culher de ray, e pausa le strument am la medicina sobre la vula, e·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu latz per so que corro saliva o musellage de la boca de aquel per la intrinscequa medicina, per so que no deyssenda de aquela deguna causa sobre le golayro de lu e que ledesca aquel.	Let the extremity of it be concave in such a way that the medicine is placed like the concavity of a spoon, and place the instrument with the medicine on the ulcer. The patient should lie on their side so that no saliva or mucus from the mouth mixes with the intrinsic medicine, so that it does not descend by any means into the throat of the patient and cause harm to them.
E aprop te la tua ma am la medicina, e exprem aquela sobre la uvula per l’espazi de miega hora entro que vegas aquela esser denegrada e sedada per la mordicacio de la medicina.	Then place your hand with the medicine and apply it to the uvula for a short period of time until you see it become darkened and soothed by the action of the medicine.
E si vols, prengues coto e envolopes aquel sobre la extremitat del ray, e submergeys le coto en la medicina, e entrometas le ray am le coto en una canula de sobre entro que·l coto adheresca en aquela canula, e fay aquo tantas vetz entro que consiegues aquo que vols de la cauterizacio de la uva, e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela se seccara e cayra aprop tres dias o quatre.	And if you wish, take some cloth and wrap it around the end of the reed, and submerge the cloth in the medicine, and insert the reed with the cloth into a tube so that the cloth adheres to that tube, and do this as many times until you achieve what you want from the cauterization of the grape, and then let it dry until it falls off after three or four days.
E si indigeysses que iteras la medicina, itera aquela, e aprop la cauterizacio abstergeys en le circuit de la uva am coto enbegut en boder, e mondifica am aquel aquo que es en le circuit de lu de la medicina, e sia lavat am aygua frega, e sia curat deforo am embrocacio, e dedintz am guarguarismes entro que sia sanat.	And if you need to repeat the medicine, do so, and then for the cauterization, clean around the grape with a cloth soaked in wine, and modify what is in its circuit of the medicine, and it should be washed with cold water, and treated externally with poultices, and internally with decoctions until it is healed.
E aquesta especia de curacio es pus salva que inscizio e pus long de temor.	And this type of treatment is safer than incision and longer in duration.
Alcunas veguadas es curada la uvuola am aquo que es pus subtil que cauteri e inscizio, quar es curat am subfumigacio en aquesta manieyra: recipe calament, ysop, origua, ruda, scicados arabic, camamilla, broyda e semblant ad aquels de las erbas, e ajusta totas aquelas causas, o alcunas de lor, en una ola, e sian submergidas am vi agre, e bulhan; e la ola sia be lutada am lut decentment, e sia en le mieg loc de la ola un trauc, sobre le qual sia pausat un instrument conquau de aram segon aquesta manieyra; sia fayt de argent o de aram.	Sometimes the uvula is cured with something more subtle than cauterization and incision, for it is treated by fumigation in this manner: take candles, hyssop, origanum, rue, saffron, chamomile, bryony, and similar herbs; prepare all those ingredients or some of them in a pot, and let them be submerged in sour wine, and boil; the pot should be well sealed with suitable wax, and place a tube in the middle of the pot on which is placed a concave instrument made of silver or iron.
E sia entromesa la extremitat en la boca del malaute entro que la vapor poge a la uvula sobre la quanula, entro que la uvula sia mot ofuscada.	And insert the extremity into the mouth of the patient so that the vapor reaches the uvula over the canal, so that the uvula is moved or obscured.
E aprop itera sobre aquela motas veguadas entro qu’es secca, e guarda te que no fassas aquesta curacio al comesament de l’aveniment de apostemas, quar trop ajustaria en le apostema, e no cove que tu fassas aquo, sino deves la declaracio de apostema de lu caut.	And then apply to those dry spotted areas, and be careful not to perform this treatment at the beginning of the occurrence of abscesses, because it would overly concentrate on the abscess, and you should not do that; instead, you should declare the treatment of the abscess with a cautery.
Mays si no es a tu present aquest instrument, lahoras pren una cana e compon en la extramitat de lu un clos de huou, per so que la boca del malaute sia comborida, quar le closc del huou prohibeys la vapor comburir la boca.	And if this instrument is not available to you, then take a reed and attach an eggshell to the end of it so that the patient's mouth can be cleaned, because the eggshell prevents the steam from burning the mouth.
E aquesta curacio es bona am salut.	And this treatment is good for health.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Chapter XXXVIII.
De extraccio d’espinas e de aquo que adhereys en le golayro e de las autras causas.	On the extraction of thorns and other objects that adhere to the throat and other causes.
Motas veguadas adhereys en le guolayro o spina de peys o alcuna autra causa.	Spotted objects adhering to the throat or fish bones or some other cause.
Adonc cove que tu extraguas aquo que de aquels es apparent, sobre le qual catz la vista, pus que tu premes la lengua am instrument denant solelh, per so que a tu sia declarat aquo que es en la guola.	Then you must extract what is visible of those objects, on which you focus your sight, by pressing the tongue with an instrument in front of light, so that you can see clearly what is in the throat.
E aquo que no apar e es a tu occultat en le guolayro, cove que tu fassas vomir le malaute denant que la vianda sia degerida en l’estomac, quar fort leu la causa annexsa le golayro sira foro-getada per vomit; o que deglusia le malaute una pessa de nap o de razit de laytuga o un boci de pa sec; o prengua una pessa de sponga marina sequa leon, e lia aquela fortment am fiel, e aprop le malaute transglussia aquela, quar cum perve al loc en le qual so spinas e es extrahuda, lahoras so foro-getatz.	And what does not appear and is hidden in the throat, you must make the patient vomit before the food is digested in the stomach, because by doing so, the cause attached to the throat will be forcefully expelled through vomiting; or that the patient swallows a piece of raw radish or chicory root or a piece of dry bread; or takes a piece of dried sea sponge, and soaks it strongly with honey, and then the patient swallows that, because when it reaches the place where thorns are and is extracted, it will be forcefully expelled.
E mays pren una anguila e be am fiel liada, e sia dedintz mesa e soptament sia extrayta; o pren un porr e soptament le metas e soptament l’en tratz.	And also take an eel and wrap it in honey, and place it inside until it is softly extracted; or take a leek and soften it and then insert it gently.
Mays si no so foro-getatz am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas, lahoras husa de un instrument de plom segon aquesta forma:	And if it is not forcefully expelled by the causes we have mentioned, then use an instrument made of lead according to this form:
E sia pus gros que ray un petit, e en la extramitat de lu sia conquavitat la qual tu entrometas en la sua guola am facilitat.	And it should be thicker than a small tube, and at one end, it should have a curvature that allows you to insert it into the patient's throat easily.
E el aga le sieu cap elevat en sus, e guarda te que·l tocament del sieu os de la gola, per so que endevengua a lu cos e am aquela que enpellesca le os o la spina, o que aquel le metge am la sua ma.	And raise the patient's head upwards, and be careful not to touch the bones of their throat, so that you do not cause harm by pushing against the bone or spine, or have the doctor use their hand to guide it.
Mays empero que·l malaute aquel entrometa es miels, per la sua sciencia del loc de la causa annexa e enpellisca en jos, e tira la sua ma am le instrument en sus, tot aquo segon la quantitat la qual es a lu preparada entro que sia foro-getada.	And although the patient himself interferes more, by his knowledge of the site of the attached cause and pushes into it, and pulls his hand with the instrument onto it, all this according to the quantity that is prepared for him inside before being plugged up.
Capitol .xxxix.	Capitol .xxxix.
De extraccio de sancguisugua annexsa al golayro.	From the extraction of the leech attached to the neck.
Quan es medicada sanguisugua am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la curacio am medicinas e no comfereys, considera lahoras en le guolayro del malaute al solelh, pus que tu aias compremuda la lengua de lu am instrument le qual a tu havem recomtat.	When leeches are treated as we have said in the section of treatment with medicines and not compresses, consider at this time the shadow of the patient under the sun, because you have examined the tongue of the patient with an instrument that we have recommended.
Donc si tu vezes la sancguisugua, extratz aquela am onci petit o am gesti subtils decentment.	Therefore, if you use bloodletting, extract it with a small instrument or with subtle maneuvers appropriately.
E si no es a tu possible estrayre am aquel, lahoras pren una canula concava e entromet aquela en lo guolayro del malaute, e aprop pausa en la concavitat de la canula un ferr ignit, e fay aquo tantas vetz (entro que la sancguisugua sia morta e se osta del guolayro) e abstengua se le malaute tot lo jorn de aygua.	And if it is not possible for you to extract with that, then take a concave cannula and insert that into the throat of the patient, and then place an ignited iron in the concavity of the cannula, and do this as many times (until the bloodsucker is dead and comes out of the throat) and the patient must abstain from water for the entire day.
E aprop prengua una veyria plena de aygua frega, e obra la boca de lu en aquela, e lava la boca am aquela; e no trasglucia de aquela alcuna causa e maugua l’aygua una hora aprop autra am la sua ma, quar la sancguisugua tantost cum sent l’aygua catz.	And then take a vessel full of cold water, open the mouth of the patient in it, and wash the mouth with it; and do not remove it for any reason and let the patient gargle the water back and forth with their hand for about an hour, because the bloodsucker immediately contracts upon feeling the water.

En le qual es la suma del sermo en apercio de apostemas e en seccio de lor.	In which is the summary of the discourse concerning abscesses and their incision.
Les apostemas so motas specias, de motas manieyras, segon que ve rememoracio de lor, de quascuna en aquest libre.	These abscesses are various types, in different ways, according to their description, each one in this book.

And other abscesses which should be treated when they are still raw and not yet fully matured, such as those near joints; for an abscess near a joint prolongs its existence until you can remove what is inside it, and this weakens or corrupts the ligaments or nerves of that joint, causing contraction of the limb. Or if it is an abscess near a major limb, and if you delay piercing it until it is fully matured, it will affect the main limb; or if it is near the buttocks, pierce it before it is fully matured; but do not puncture one that is raw or incompletely digested, except for those near the buttocks, so as to prevent its pus from spreading inside the buttocks and forming a fistula, or becoming incurable at the site.

And you must know that it is matured when there is the cessation of pain and the end of fever, and also the reduction of heat and pulsation, and the sharpness at the head of the abscess, and other signs.

De seccio del pilhot del apostema accident dintz le guolayro.	Of the section of the abscess plug that occurs in the groin.
Diyssero les antics aquesta seccio en le epilhot, e no vist alcu hom en nostra terra que aquela aia fayta.	The ancients performed this section on the abscess plug, and no one has been seen in our land who has done this procedure.
E aquesta es la inscriptura del sermo de aquels.	And this is the inscription of the speech of those [individuals].
