Donc cove quan volem aquo, que inscidam le epilhot dejos tres cercles dels cercles del epilhot, o quatre am petita seccio per la latitut en aquel que es entre dos cercles per quantitat, que la seccio sia en ciphac, no en la cartillage, e aquest loc es convenent a seccio, quar es privat de carn e les vayselhs de sanc de lu son luhen.	Therefore, when we want to do this, we must incise the epididymis leaving three circles of the epididymis untouched, or make four small sections across its width between two such circles, ensuring that the cut is made in the body part, not in the cartilage, and this area is suitable for sectioning because it lacks flesh and the blood vessels are sparse.
E si le metge es pauruc, cove lahoras que extenda la codena del golayro am onci, e aprop fenda la codena entro que pervengua a la canal, mays evite les vaysels de sanc si vetz de aquelas alcuna causa.	And if the doctor is inexperienced, it is necessary to extend the ligament of the kneecap with an incision, and then cut the ligament until it reaches the canal, but avoid the blood vessels if there is any reason to do so.
E aprop inscida li ciplach segon que havem recomtat; e es significat sobre la seccio de la canal per le flacma le qual es de aquela eyssit am aquo que es de lu disromput e per la abscizio de la votz.	Then incise the chipla as we have recommended; it is indicated by the section of the canal through the flap, which is that part that remains after the disruption and by the separation of the voice. 
E layssa la plagua uberta per alcun temps.	And leave the wound open for some time.
Donc cum la hora es remauguda en la qual perforacio es temuda, agregua doas labias de la codena de la plagua, e cus aquela sola ses la cartillage.	When the hour is dreaded in which the perforation is feared, add two loops of the chain of the wound, and thus only the cartilage is affected. 
E aprop administra medicinas que fan naysser la carn entro que sia sanat.	And then administer medicines that promote flesh growth within so that it may heal.
E diyssec Albucasis que la summa del sermo le qual havem recomtat, exposicio no es sino que veias que alcus de aquetz apostemas ja han opilat lo guolayro del malaute, e le malaute es vengut entro a mort, e le ale de lu es entresecat, e alcus van a inscidir le epiglos per so que respire le malaute sobre le loc de la plagua per alcuna respiracio, e sia salvat de mort.	And Albucasis says that the essence of the sermon we have recounted is that some of those abscesses have already obstructed the windpipe of the patient, and the patient has come near to death, and their breath is cut off, and some proceed to incise the epiglottis so that the patient may breathe at the site of the wound through some respiration and be saved from death.
E per aquo comandero layssar la plagua uberta entro que sia consumida la malicia de la malautia; e es la malicia de lu per tres dias; e donc lahoras comandero cosi la plagua, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And by this, you should leave the wound open until the malignity of the disease is consumed; and the malignity lasts for three days; and then after that, you should close the wound and treat it until it heals.
E aquo que yeu he vist per mi meteys, es que una sirventa pres un cotel e mesec le en le sieu golayro e inscidic am aquel una partida de la cana del pulmo, e yeu fu apelat a la curacio de lu, e atrobegui la mugen ayssi cum es mugit del moridos, e descubrigui la plagua e atrobegui le sanc le qual era yssit de la plagua petit.	And what I have seen in my practice is that a servant took a knife and inserted it into her windpipe and cut a part of the trachea with it, and I was called for her treatment, and I found the sound like the moaning of someone dying, and uncovered the wound and found blood that had seeped from the small wound.
Donc yeu fo confessat que aquela no havia inscidit vena ni guidegi, e le vent yssia de la plagua, e curegui aquela entro que foc sanada.	Therefore, it must be confessed that she had not cut any vein or artery, and the air came out of the wound, and she treated it until it healed.
E no accidic a la sirventa si no rauquiera en la votz, e aprop alcus dias retornec ad miloracio de las suas dispozicios.	And it does not harm the servant if there is no hoarseness in their voice, and after a few days they return to the improvement of their conditions.
E ara dic yeu que en la seccio del epilhot no ha temor.	And now I say that in the section of the hernia there is no fear.

Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De seccio de las specias de nodes.	On the section of types of nodes.
Dels nodes so motas specias e yeu ja he dit totas las specias de lor en la divisio.	About the various types of nodes, I have already described all their types in the division.

Donc yeu dic que am exitura es caliditat e febre e dolors vehementz entro que es sedada la ebullicio de la superfluitat; e es complida putrefaccio que lahora cessa la febre, la dolor e la calor.	So I say that in a hernia there is heat and fever and violent pains within until the boiling of the excess is calmed; and complete putrefaction occurs at which point the fever, pain, and heat cease.
Mays am node no es caliditat ni febre ni dolor, e conte aquel ciphac leon le qual es al u sac propri.	However, in a knot, there is neither heat nor fever nor pain, and it contains a solid mass that is like a lion's paw in its own sack.
E es segon la color del cors, e le comensament de lu es cum un ceze e es fayt ayssi cum vace, sia major o minor, e son segon dos specias, quar o so grassas e conteno humiditat, e las colors de la humiditat son motas, segon que yeu diyssi en la divisio. And it is the method of investigating abscesses and all knots, which is that you take this tool and insert it into the most moist area that you find in the abscess, and you will stir the contents with it little by little until you know that the tool has penetrated the core.

ayssi cum t’e ensenhat, e suspen aquel am oncis, e excorja la codena de tota part am facilitat, e guarda la pel o sac, si podes, sobre aquel e extraguas aquela sania am le node. Mays si es romput en la operacio, no es possible extrayre aquela sana, e motas veguadas endeve aquo, e lahoras tu la extratz a pessas entro que de lu no romangua denguna causa.	But if it is broken during the operation, it is not possible to extract that pus entirely, and sometimes you must do this instead, and then you extract it in pieces to ensure nothing remains.
Quar si de lu roman denguna causa, pauc o trop, le node retorne segon le mays.	For if any of it remains, whether little or much, the knot will return accordingly.

And if you see that some small part remains from it, then complete the wound with some sharp and caustic powders, strengthen the wound, place over where the abscess sits a cautery, and treat that with another form of cure until it is healed.
E si es node gran, lahoras tu cus las doas labias de lu e cura aquel am aquo que encarna.	And if the knot is large, then sew the two lips of it together and treat that with something that promotes healing.
Mays si vena pulsatil es a lu contraria, o no-pulsatil, lahoras tu coyta e huemple le loc de zegi trissat que es vetriol e leyssa aquel streyt per dos dias o per tres entro que·s poyresca la plagua e que repause la ebullicio del sanc; e aprop retorna a inscindir aquo que es romas del node. Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De seccio de apostemas que accideysso per arceria o per vena.	On the section of abscesses that occur due to arteries or veins.

The signs by which it is known that inflammation and abscess are due to an artery or a vein: for when the abscess is due to an artery, it forms a long aggregation in the area of the body; and when you press the abscess with your fingers, you feel a rustling sound within it.

Mays sobre aquel que es de lor per imflacio de l’orrifici de la arceria, scindeys en la codena seccio en le lonc; e aprop huebre la seccio am uncis e aprop la arceria, e deliura de las tunicas entro que sia descuberta.	And for that which is caused by the inflammation of the artery orifice, make a longitudinal incision along the cord; then widen the incision with forceps and approach the artery, and free it from the tunics so that it is exposed.
E aprop met sobre aquel agulha e fay aquela penetrar entro al autre latz, e estrenh la arceria am fiel doble en dos locs, — la qual causa yeu a tu eyssenhegui en extraccio de doas arcerias les quals so en les templars.	And then place the needle and make it penetrate to the other side, and tie the artery with double thread in two places — this method is useful for you to learn in the extraction of two arteries which are in the temples.
E aprop punh le loc le qual es entre dos liamentz am spatum entro que yesca le sanc tot que es en lu, e sia dissolvut le apostema.	And then separate the area between two ligaments with a spatula until all the blood that is in it has come out, and the swelling is thus dissolved.
E aprop administra curacio en la qual es engendrat poyre entro que caian les liamentz; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz convenientz ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And then administer treatment in which pus is generated where the ligaments are inflamed; and then treat it with appropriate ointments until it is healed.
E si es apostema per seccio de vena, lahoras cove que tu tenguas am la tua ma aquo que es a tu possible del apostema am la codena, e aprop intromet la agulha dejos le loc le qual tu has tengut dejos la tua ma, e fay aquela penetrar; e sia en aquela fil doble entro que tu extraguas aquel del autre latz, e aprop ligua le apostema am bo liament segon que yeu he dit a tu en le liament de uva4 de doas partz am doas extremitatz del fil.	And if the abscess is due to vein constriction, then you must hold with your hand as much of the abscess as possible with a ligature, and then insert the needle into the place where you have held with your hand; make it penetrate; and use that double thread until you pull it out from the other side, and then tie off the abscess with a strong bandage as I have said to you in the vein binding of both sides with both ends of the thread.
Mays si temes que extraguam le fil, lahoras entromet le fiel am aquela agula dejos tot le apostema deves la inscizio de la agulha primieyra, e strenh les tieus fiels en quatre locs.	And if you fear that the thread might be pulled out, then insert the thread with that needle throughout the abscess leaving the tip of the needle first, and secure the threads at four places.
Aprop secca le apostema en le mieg loc de lu entro que quan es yssit aquo que es en lu, lahoras tu inscideys la superfluitat de la codena, e layssa aquo que de lu es liat.	Then dry the abscess in its middle until what is inside it is removed; then you cut off the excess of the ligature, leaving what is tied.
E aprop pausa sobre lu pulvil le qual has submergit en vi e oli, e aprop administra la curacio la qual es fayta am calguas e enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then place over it a cushion that you have soaked in wine and oil, and then administer the treatment made with plasters and ointments until it is healed.
Capitol l del apostema le qual accideys per torcio de nervis.	Capitulize the abscess which you encounter due to nerve twisting.
Ayssi cum accideys apostema en arceria e en vena, e semblantment accideys apostema en les nervis quan accideys en lor percussio o accideys per trebal superfluable, e per semblantz.	Here is the translation of the provided sentence:
E es fayt le mays de lu en les locs dels adjutoris o del talo, o en tot loc en le qual so maugudas las juncturas.	And the incision is made in the areas of the instep or the ankle, or in any place where the joints are painful.
E es apostema greu, e es asemblat a la color del autre cors, e es en las majors de lu disposicios ses de lor e quan es streyt am vehementia, sent en lu le malaute semblant stupor.	And it is a severe abscess, and it resembles the color of the rest of the body, and it occurs in the major parts of the body where such conditions are disposed to occur, and when it becomes tight with vehemence, the patient appears to be in a state of stupor.
E no es apostema agreguat en le preon del cors, e per so es dejos la codena, e el es maugut a tota partida e no va a las partidas denant ni detras.	And it is not an aggregated abscess in the groin area of the body, and therefore the chain (likely referring to lymph nodes or muscles) is left behind, and it spreads throughout without moving forward or backward.
Donc aquo de aquels que es en las juncturas no cove que sia envasit am ferr, quar fort leu endevenguera contracio.	Therefore, of those that are in the joints, it is not necessary to wrap them with iron, for fear that they will cause contraction.
Mays aquel que es en le cap o en le front fen la codena am spatum.	But those that are on the head or forehead should be treated with a spatum (likely a type of medical instrument).
Mays si es apostema pauc, lahoras te aquel am les forfecs e abscindeys aquel de razitz.	But if it is a small abscess, then take hold of it with forceps and remove it completely.
E si es gran, lahoras tu le suspen am unci, e excorja aquel, e aprop osta aquel; e ajusta la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if it is large, then suspend it with an incision, and drain it, and then clean the area; sew up the wound, and care for it until it heals.

De seccio de apostema le qual accideys de cheil que accideys al ventre.	Of the incision of an abscess that occurs from the groin to the abdomen. 
Endeveno ad alcus homes motas veguadas en les ventres de aquels e en las autras partidas del cors de aquels theils les quals son apelatz funguals per similitut de aquels am funges, dels quals la razitz es subtil e·l cap de aquel es gros; e ja las labias de aquels so conversas, e es de aquels que es petit, e es de aquels que es mot magnificat.
